\DoxyCodeLine{00715\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ We\ don't\ want\ to\ require\ the\ users\ to\ write\ TypesN<...>\ directly,}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00719\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ argument,\ even\ if\ it\ has\ the\ default\ value\ (this\ means\ Types<int>}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00720\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ will\ appear\ as\ Types<int,\ None,\ None,\ ...,\ None>\ in\ the\ compiler}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00721\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ errors).}}
